SELECT q."Id", q."AuthorId", q."DateOfCreation", q."DateOfUpdate", q."Description", q."Rating", q."Title", u."Id", s."QuestionId", s."TagId", s."Id", s."Name", u."PasswordHash", u."Rating", u."UserEmail", u."UserName"
FROM "Questions" AS q
INNER JOIN "Users" AS u ON q."AuthorId" = u."Id"
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT q0."QuestionId", q0."TagId", t."Id", t."Name"
    FROM "QuestionTag" AS q0
    INNER JOIN "Tags" AS t ON q0."TagId" = t."Id"
) AS s ON q."Id" = s."QuestionId"
ORDER BY q."Id", u."Id", s."QuestionId", s."TagId"
